[λ°•μ„ΈνΈ] [μ¤ν›„ 4:33] I would like to let you know that as usual whenever you visit KKBSC before you leave you always contribute to the school. This time if you still have a plan to contribute, you can give to the 40 Years Thanksgiving program and graduation day that will be held on March 16. and 17, 2024. This is my kind suggestion for the team. 

Pastor Joshua, Pastor Sam, you and I will meet someday soon. We will plan for a special trip to Kawthoolei. Based on the ground level, God opens the big door or larger space for us to cross over to the other side. We will visit regional, and central leaders in Kawthoolei. We will explore more opportunities to develop God's kingdom in Kawthoolei. We already spent many years in the Refugee camp, in Thailand. 2024 and 25 get ready to cross over to the other side, Kawthoolei. I have a dream one day, we can go back and reestablish our new life once again in Kawthoolri, Karen Land which God has given to the Katen people. Let us Make Kawthoolri great again!

[λ°•μ„ΈνΈ] [μ¤ν›„ 1:39] Greetings Letter to KEEN Ministry

Dear Pastor Seth Park,
Greetings to you in the Name of our Lord and Savior Jesus Christ!

First and foremost, I would like to extend my heartfelt greetings and sincere gratitude to you, the leadership team, and all members of the KEEN Ministry. Your faithful service and unwavering commitment have been a tremendous blessing to the Karen community, particularly to the Kaawthoolei Karen Baptist Bible School and College.
As we approach the special occasion of the Mo Woo Da Worship in April 2025, I earnestly pray that the sovereignty of our Almighty God will continue to sustain your lives, expand your vision, and empower all pastors and leaders involved in KEEN Ministry. May your efforts to advance the Kingdom of God in this 21st century be more effective than ever, guided by the Spirit and grounded in faith.
Let us awaken the nations through fervent prayer, heartfelt worship, and a steadfast commitment to proclaiming the Gospel. I pray that all KEEN ministers, pastors, leaders, and members will be united in purpose, driven by compassion, and wholly devoted to glorifying God.

Hope is alive.

In His Service,

Dr. Saw Alwyn
President
Global Kawthoolei Karen Baptist Bible School & College

We Karen people live in the camp  too long already.

Dependecy is a poison..

Therefore, we have seek and try to get kawhoolei as a independence state for the Karen people.

Then, Karen people can go back and workout by themselves freely with integrity.

I already prepared a curriculum for the UK. Kawhoolei University. We need a keen ministry to play a major role for the UK.

We need transformative leaders to change the living condition of the Karen people.

I hope you can share this vision for UK to your team.
